# Image Sourcing Plan

This file helps replace reused reference images without deleting the existing image pool.

## `vsec_001`

- domain: `visual_security`
- task_category: `rigid_body_kinematics_and_coupling`
- current_image_path: `dataset/images/construction/veh_014.jpg`
- current_image_reuse_count: `5`
- scenario: forklift overspeed during a tight turn causing pallet cargo to slide outward under centrifugal force.
- requirement: Use a clear industrial photo with visible joints, rigid links, axes, supports, load path, tool contact, or coupled mechanism geometry.
- recommended_search_query: `forklift overspeed during a tight turn causing pallet cargo to slide outward under centrifugal force. industrial security surveillance restricted zone worker ppe forklift vehicle intrusion rigid body kinematics and coupling real industrial photo high resolution`
- local_candidate_images: `dataset/images/construction/veh_014.jpg | dataset/images/aerospace/wide_body_aircraft_belly_view.jpg | dataset/images/construction/road_train_coupling_system.jpg | dataset/images/manufacturing/industrial_washing_line.jpg | dataset/images/maritime/cargo_ship.jpg`

```text
Use the provided reference image as the first frame and visual anchor. Generate a 5-8 second realistic industrial video. Scene: forklift overspeed during a tight turn causing pallet cargo to slide outward under centrifugal force. Reference subject: veh 014. Camera: perform a smooth constant-radius orbit around the subject; target motion value 45.0. Action: Show the rigid mechanism moving under load with all links, joints, tools, supports, and contact points staying physically coupled. Keep the same equipment identity, layout, colors, materials, background, and perspective cues from the reference image. Do not add text overlays, subtitles, logos, watermarks, extra machines, or unrelated people. Avoid melting, flicker, identity swaps, component-count changes, impossible floating loads, rigid-body bending, and accidental global scene changes.
```
